    window.RLQ.push(function () {
        function genUID() {
            return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
                var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);

                return v.toString(16);
            });
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            var cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');

            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        var beacon = getCookieValue('wikia_beacon_id');
        var sessionId = getCookieValue('tracking_session_id');
        var pvNumber = getCookieValue('pv_number');
        var pvNumberGlobal = getCookieValue('pv_number_global');
        var expireDate = new Date(Date.now() + 1000 * 60 * 30);

        mw.config.set({
            sessionId: sessionId ? sessionId : genUID(),
            pvNumber: pvNumber ? parseInt(pvNumber, 10) + 1 : 1,
            pvNumberGlobal: pvNumberGlobal ? parseInt(pvNumberGlobal, 10) + 1 : 1,
            pvUID: genUID(),
            beaconId: beacon
        });

        document.cookie = 'tracking_session_id=' + mw.config.get('sessionId') + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
                ';domain=' + mw.config.get('wgCookieDomain') + '; path=' + mw.config.get('wgCookiePath') + ';';
        document.cookie = 'pv_number=' + mw.config.get('pvNumber') + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
                '; path=' + mw.config.get('wgScriptPath') + ';';
        document.cookie = 'pv_number_global=' + mw.config.get('pvNumberGlobal') + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
                ';domain=' + mw.config.get('wgCookieDomain') + '; path=' + mw.config.get('wgCookiePath') + ';';
    });
</script>

															<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
    (function () {
        // we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
        var videoDetails = {
            mediaId: "uiEwVzB5",
            impressionsPerSession: 1,
            isDedicatedForArticle: true,
        };
        var hasVideoOnPage = null;
        var videoBridgeCountries = ["US","CA","AU"];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            var cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
            var impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
            var allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

            if (!hasSeenTheVideoInCurrentSession()) {
                return false;
            }

            if (allowedImpressions === 0) {
                return true;
            }

            return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
        }

        function hasSeenTheVideoInCurrentSession() {
            var currentSession = getCookieValue('wikia_session_id');
            var videoSeenInSession = getCookieValue('featuredVideoSeenInSession');

            return currentSession && videoSeenInSession && currentSession === videoSeenInSession;
        }

        function getCountryCode() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
            var countryCode = getCountryCode();
            var allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
                return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
            });

            return countryCode && allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
        }

        window.canPlayVideo = function () {
            if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
                hasVideoOnPage = videoDetails.mediaId && (
                    videoDetails.isDedicatedForArticle ||
	                (!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() && isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry())
                );
            }

            return hasVideoOnPage;
        };

        if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
            document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
        } else {
	        document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
        }
    })();
</script>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="kanji">

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">個性</div>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background">First Appearance</h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="debut">

		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Manga Debut</h3>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Chapter_1" title="Chapter 1">Chapter 1</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="debutanime">

		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Anime Debut</h3>

	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Episode_1" title="Episode 1">Episode 1</a></div>

</p><p>A <b>Quirk</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">個性</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kosei</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, lit. "Individuality")</span>, also known as a <b>Meta Ability</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">異能</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Inō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> by the <a href="/wiki/Meta_Liberation_Army" title="Meta Liberation Army">Meta Liberation Army</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-auto-a952a157594c22c372a2c9316815c962_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-a952a157594c22c372a2c9316815c962-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> is a special, superhuman ability that a person can have.
</p><p>Along with being unique to each user, Quirks are compartmentalized into multiple categories. Quirk users are also limited to one ability and are thus unable to achieve any other.
</p>

<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10"><a href="#Quirk_Types"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Quirk Types</span></a>
<ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/1b/Luminescent_Baby_%28Anime%29.png/revision/latest?cb=20170701230929" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/1b/Luminescent_Baby_%28Anime%29.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170701230929" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luminescent Baby (Anime).png" data-image-key="Luminescent_Baby_(Anime).png" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luminescent_Baby_(Anime).png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The first Quirk.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The first person in the world to manifest a Quirk was a <a href="/wiki/Luminescent_Baby" title="Luminescent Baby">newborn baby</a> in <a href="/wiki/Qing_Qing_City,_China" title="Qing Qing City, China">Qing Qing City, China</a>; the baby had the ability to emanate light from their body.
</p><p>After that phenomenon, many people around the world began to manifest different kinds of superpowers. While the cause of the Quirk phenomenon is unknown, it has been theorized that the development of Quirks was caused by the spread of a virus carried by mice. These superpowers were first referred to as Meta Abilities before later being called Quirks.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-a06760af94100b092d29b574d5807dd5_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-a06760af94100b092d29b574d5807dd5-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c166p6_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c166p6-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The dawn of this extraordinary era was marred by a breakdown of society caused by the sudden onslaught of criminals empowered by their newfound "superpowers" and ordinary people being prejudiced against the Quirk users.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/f/f9/Dawn_of_Vigilantes.png/revision/latest?cb=20190927095907" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/f/f9/Dawn_of_Vigilantes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190927095907" decoding="async" width="220" height="204" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dawn of Vigilantes.png" data-image-key="Dawn_of_Vigilantes.png" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dawn_of_Vigilantes.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The era of Vigilantes.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As chaos and unrest ensued due to the outbreak of Quirks, ordinary civilians with their own Quirks decided to take matters into their own hands to bring order to society and thus the first "Heroes" appeared in the form of <a href="/wiki/Vigilantes" title="Vigilantes">Vigilantes</a> and thus beginning the Vigilantes Era.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During this time period, <a href="/wiki/All_For_One" title="All For One">All For One</a> became a symbol of unity in society. He used his <a href="/wiki/All_For_One_(Quirk)" title="All For One (Quirk)">Quirk</a> to remove Quirks from those who did not want them and give Quirks to those that did. His actions under the guise of returning society to its prior state of humanity, when in reality, he was gathering followers who were loyal to him, allowing him to act out his ulterior motives.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-ff3ff1ed935e962a48ae0ee14fef42ad_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-ff3ff1ed935e962a48ae0ee14fef42ad-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As society adapted to the new status quo, the <a href="/wiki/Police_Force" title="Police Force">Police Force</a> moved to prioritize leadership and to maintain the status quo, and as such, decided not to use Quirks as weapons. To fill that void, the profession of crime-fighting Quirk users, <a href="/wiki/Heroes" title="Heroes">Pro Heroes</a>, began to exist which caused the Vigilantes to slowly disappear. Authorizing the use of powers that could so easily kill, however, was a greatly criticized decision at first.
</p><p>Over time, it came to garner public support due to the fact that the first people to work professionally as heroes acted morally and upheld the law.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-bfc866a76ba87628356c460f5ffbd72e_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-bfc866a76ba87628356c460f5ffbd72e-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> However, some members of society were not happy with the governments' regulations on Quirk usage as they believed that the free use of their superhuman abilities should be a basic human right.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-91a6d531c2830eed2e974e01af9ace19_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-91a6d531c2830eed2e974e01af9ace19-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A group of Quirk users known as the <a href="/wiki/Meta_Liberation_Army" title="Meta Liberation Army">Meta Liberation Army</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Chikara_Yotsubashi" title="Chikara Yotsubashi">Destro</a>, had tried to stop the passing of regulations that would restrict Quirk usage. They rebelled against the governments of a number of nations for several years before ultimately suffering defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-473b4394be6a5f7fdbb470c83ad3cc01_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-473b4394be6a5f7fdbb470c83ad3cc01-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Currently, roughly 80% of the people who make up the global population possess a Quirk.<sup id="cite_ref-c1p4_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1p4-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Information">Information</span></h2>
<p>Quirks are said to be the next stage of evolution in the human race. It is possible to diagnose a person as possessing or lacking a Quirk by analyzing the presence or absence of an extra joint in their pinky toe. People with only one joint will develop a Quirk while having two joints indicates that the person is <a href="/wiki/Quirkless" title="Quirkless">Quirkless</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1p19_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1p19-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A person's Quirk will normally manifest around the age of four years old, although, it is possible for a child to be born with their Quirks already manifested, such was the case with <a href="/wiki/Hizashi_Yamada" title="Hizashi Yamada">Present Mic</a><sup id="cite_ref-auto-0993e1d2eb20c1f5e41c5e4ca1b9669d_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-0993e1d2eb20c1f5e41c5e4ca1b9669d-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and the very first person to manifest a Quirk, the <a href="/wiki/Luminescent_Baby" title="Luminescent Baby">Luminescent Baby</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1p4_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1p4-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/a/ad/Shoto_frostbite.png/revision/latest?cb=20170730181802" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/a/ad/Shoto_frostbite.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170730181802" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shoto frostbite.png" data-image-key="Shoto_frostbite.png" /></a> 	 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shoto_frostbite.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shoto's overuse of his Quirk gives him frostbite.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Although easy to forget, the fact is that Quirks are physical abilities. As such, they can be trained and worn out. When a person works out their muscles, the muscle fibers are destroyed and new, stronger ones grow back; this same rule applies to Quirks. However, should a Quirk be overused, the user could suffer any of a variety of drawbacks, depending on the nature of the Quirk. These drawbacks are usually simple ailments, such as dry skin or nausea; however, in some cases, the drawback can be much more severe.
</p><p>There are also instances where a Quirk doesn't suit the user's body and the body can't handle it. Some people, such as <a href="/wiki/Yuga_Aoyama" title="Yuga Aoyama">Yuga Aoyama</a>, suffer from birth defects that cause the victim to have difficulties controlling their <a href="/wiki/Navel_Laser" title="Navel Laser">Quirk</a>. Such conditions can be bypassed through the use of support equipment, such as <a href="/wiki/Yuga_Aoyama#Equipment" title="Yuga Aoyama">Yuga's belt</a>. Similarly, <a href="/wiki/Nine" title="Nine">Nine</a> suffers from chronic pain and cellular degeneration due to the massive strain of his Quirk, <a href="/wiki/Weather_Manipulation" title="Weather Manipulation">Weather Manipulation</a>.
</p><p>Quirk levels can be measured, though only <a href="/wiki/Toshinori_Yagi" title="Toshinori Yagi">Toshinori Yagi</a>'s have ever been shown, being at 15,000 AP at his peak and reaching a low point of 2,500 AP in the present.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-3e2d1b505ce43ca5661969356203b4a3_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-3e2d1b505ce43ca5661969356203b4a3-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although very rare, it is also possible for animals to possess Quirks, such as <a href="/wiki/Nezu" title="Nezu">Nezu</a> having a Quirk that gives him <a href="/wiki/High_Spec" title="High Spec">above-human intelligence</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-79d8f7c8e2566e9adf0a76dd550c5931_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-79d8f7c8e2566e9adf0a76dd550c5931-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Every Quirk contains an echo of the consciousness of its wielder; if a person's Quirk is transferred to someone else, the consciousness of the previous wielder will appear in the new user's mind, either as voices in dreams or manifestations in a mental mindscape. If further transferred to yet another new user, then that new user will experience the consciousnesses of all of the previous users. Though, these consciousnesses will disappear if the new user loses the transferred Quirk.<sup id="cite_ref-c287_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c287-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Factor">Quirk Factor</span></h3>
<p>The term "Quirk Factor"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">個性因子</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kosei Inshi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, lit. "Individuality Factor")</span> refers to the collective physical and genetic traits that compose a person's Quirk. This includes the primary Quirk power as well as all the biological mechanisms that allow said primary power to function properly. Quirk Factors also contain a person's consciousness.<sup id="cite_ref-c287_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c287-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Under <a href="/wiki/All_For_One_(Quirk)" title="All For One (Quirk)">special circumstances</a>, a second Quirk can be added to a person's genetics. There is a chance that the two Quirks may merge, becoming a new Quirk, as was the case with <a href="/wiki/One_For_All" title="One For All">One For All</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-957fdd2b42d2613614bb131e58212539_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-957fdd2b42d2613614bb131e58212539-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Certain Quirks, such as <a href="/wiki/Erasure" title="Erasure">Erasure</a>, are capable of temporarily halting the expression of the Quirk Factor, rendering the Quirk unusable for a short period, but not affecting the Quirk Factor otherwise. There are other Quirks, however, that are able to directly damage the Quirk Factor of a target, preventing the Quirk from being activated until the user manages to naturally recover. It's also possible that a Quirk Factor can be damaged beyond recovery, causing the Quirk to be permanently suppressed.
</p><p>The first instance was when <a href="/wiki/Shota_Aizawa" title="Shota Aizawa">Eraser Head</a> was severely injured by the <a href="/wiki/Nomu_(U.S.J.)" title="Nomu (U.S.J.)">U.S.J. Nomu</a>. Eraser Head’s body sustained a large amount of damage, especially his face and head, and this caused his Erasure Quirk to have a much shorter time limit, as he has to blink more often because of the damage he took.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Heredity">Heredity</span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6c/Quirk_Lineage.png/revision/latest?cb=20180207190001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="137" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Quirk Lineage.png" data-image-key="Quirk_Lineage.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6c/Quirk_Lineage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180207190001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6c/Quirk_Lineage.png/revision/latest?cb=20180207190001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6c/Quirk_Lineage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180207190001" decoding="async" width="220" height="137" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Quirk Lineage.png" data-image-key="Quirk_Lineage.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6c/Quirk_Lineage.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180207190001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Quirk_Lineage.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An example of Quirk heritage of two families.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Quirks are inherited genetically through what appears to be <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mendelian_inheritance" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mendelian inheritance">Mendelian inheritance</a>. A child will either inherit the father's Quirk, the mother's Quirk, or a new composite Quirk formed by a fusion of the two. This composite Quirk may sometimes give the appearance of the person having two separate Quirks, such as <a href="/wiki/Shoto_Todoroki" title="Shoto Todoroki">Shoto Todoroki</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Half-Cold_Half-Hot" title="Half-Cold Half-Hot">Half-Cold Half-Hot</a>.
</p><p>Much more rarely, in the case of <a href="/wiki/Eri" title="Eri">Eri</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Rewind" title="Rewind">Rewind</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tomura_Shigaraki" title="Tomura Shigaraki">Tomura Shigaraki</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Decay" title="Decay">Decay</a>, a child may manifest a Quirk that is entirely unrelated to their genetic lineage, akin to a mutation.
</p><p>Physical abnormalities caused by Quirks can be passed on to the next generation, even if the Quirk that causes the abnormality is not passed on; <a href="/wiki/Fumikage_Tokoyami" title="Fumikage Tokoyami">Fumikage Tokoyami</a> has a bird-like head that has nothing to do with his <a href="/wiki/Dark_Shadow" title="Dark Shadow">shadow monster Quirk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Koji_Koda" title="Koji Koda">Koji Koda</a> has a jagged, rock-like head that has nothing to do with his power to <a href="/wiki/Anivoice" title="Anivoice">talk to animals</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mina_Ashido" title="Mina Ashido">Mina Ashido</a> has a pair of horns and eyes with black sclera instead of white, that has nothing to do with her power to <a href="/wiki/Acid" title="Acid">produce acid</a>.
</p><p>There is also a possibility that two people with Quirks will have a Quirkless child, such was the case with Izuku Midoriya.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Marriage">Quirk Marriage</span></h4>
<p>Since Quirks are passed on from parent to child, some people choose a marriage partner based on their Quirk. This is what's known as a <a href="/wiki/Quirk_Marriages" title="Quirk Marriages">Quirk Marriage</a>.
</p><p>The idea is for the child to have a powerful Quirk that combines the parents' Quirks.  A popular example of this is <a href="/wiki/Shoto_Todoroki" title="Shoto Todoroki">Shoto Todoroki</a> and his Quirk, <a href="/wiki/Half-Cold_Half-Hot" title="Half-Cold Half-Hot">Half-Cold Half-Hot</a> which is a combination of his father's Quirk, <a href="/wiki/Hellflame" title="Hellflame">Hellflame</a> and his mother, <a href="/wiki/Rei_Todoroki" title="Rei Todoroki">Rei Todoroki</a>'s ice Quirk. Powerful combinations are not guaranteed, even from strong parents - Shoto was the only one of four siblings to have a powerful combination of the parental quirks without downsides.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Frequency">Quirk Frequency</span></h3>
<p>Some Quirks are very common, in that many people possess Quirks that fall in that particular classification. Known classifications of common Quirks include:
</p>
<ul><li><b>Gigantification:</b> Quirks that allow the user to increase the size of ones self.</li></ul>
<p>Other Quirks are very rare, in that not many people possess Quirks of that nature. Known classifications of "Rare Quirks" include:
</p>
<ul><li><b>Warping</b>: Quirks that allow the user to teleport themself, other people, and/or objects to a different location.</li>
<li><b>Regeneration</b>: Quirks that allow the user to heal from severe damage quickly.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Awakening">Awakening</span></h3>
<p>After initial Quirk manifestation, it is possible for the user to undergo an "Awakening". The right catalyst can cause Quirks to evolve on the spot.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-05ef9a82e3eab295abb946c0364354fa_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-05ef9a82e3eab295abb946c0364354fa-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> This results in ones Quirk gaining a new level of strength and/or new aspects to its nature that were previously not possible.
</p><p>An example of this phenomenon is demonstrated when Himiko Toga's <a href="/wiki/Transform" title="Transform">disguise Quirk</a> evolved in a <a href="/wiki/Himiko_Toga_vs._Chitose_Kizuki" title="Himiko Toga vs. Chitose Kizuki">life-or-death situation</a>, giving her the ability to duplicate the Quirks of the people she transformed into, shown when she used <a href="/wiki/Zero_Gravity" title="Zero Gravity">Zero Gravity</a> while she had taken the form of <a href="/wiki/Ochaco_Uraraka" title="Ochaco Uraraka">Ochaco Uraraka</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-7aabe0ade71be2c81cf79d5132feba15_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-7aabe0ade71be2c81cf79d5132feba15-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> It is also said that <a href="/wiki/Geten" title="Geten">Geten</a>'s Quirk evolved when <a href="/wiki/Rikiya_Yotsubashi" title="Rikiya Yotsubashi">Re-Destro</a> burned himself, from solely the manipulation of ice to being also able to change its temperature.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-b33cd12f92135428f36155930829bfa8_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-b33cd12f92135428f36155930829bfa8-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Singularity"><a href="/wiki/Quirk_Singularity" title="Quirk Singularity">Quirk Singularity</a></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/0/03/Episode_79.png/revision/latest?cb=20200203151600" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Episode 79.png" data-image-key="Episode_79.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/0/03/Episode_79.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200203151600" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/0/03/Episode_79.png/revision/latest?cb=20200203151600" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/0/03/Episode_79.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200203151600" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Episode 79.png" data-image-key="Episode_79.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/0/03/Episode_79.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20200203151600" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Episode_79.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The next generation possessing stronger Quirks.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The theory of "Quirk Singularity" is a popular line of thinking that suggests that Quirks will continue to mix together and deepen, growing in both strength and complexity with every new generation. Eventually, Quirks will develop to a point where no one will be able to control them anymore.<sup id="cite_ref-c166p6_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c166p6-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This idea was first theorized by <a href="/wiki/Kyudai_Garaki" title="Kyudai Garaki">Kyudai Garaki</a>, who started to see early signs of this phenomenon among the fourth generation of Quirk users. However, with the exception of <a href="/wiki/All_For_One" title="All For One">All For One</a>, no one believed his theory, and he was ostracized from society as a result.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-d9d4e138ced5f8a5ce6fe0579f75150e_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-d9d4e138ced5f8a5ce6fe0579f75150e-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>This theory is first mentioned by <a href="/wiki/Seiji_Shishikura" title="Seiji Shishikura">Seiji Shishikura</a> when Present Mic notes how the <a href="/wiki/Masegaki_Primary_School" title="Masegaki Primary School">Masegaki Primary School</a> students have very powerful Quirks and have much better control over them than he did at that age.
</p><p>As mentioned by Present Mic, in the current era, this theory is viewed as fringe thinking, and is followed by some cultists.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-366c6a438fc7d4c7ef37bd13644ee30a_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-366c6a438fc7d4c7ef37bd13644ee30a-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Restriction_Laws">Quirk Restriction Laws</span></h3>
<p>In an effort to preserve order in the superhuman society, there are several laws and procedures in place to ensure the conscientious use of Quirks. Public display of Quirks is against the law,<sup id="cite_ref-auto-13d3478d9e3d2ae4790e22e8e86fbd1e_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-13d3478d9e3d2ae4790e22e8e86fbd1e-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> except in cases of self-defense, such as when one is under attack or preventing someone else from being attacked.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-cbe10d57369d3de7b111eea4aabc2aea_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-cbe10d57369d3de7b111eea4aabc2aea-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During elementary school, children receive Quirk counseling in order to learn how to use their powers responsibly.<sup id="cite_ref-auto-ad95e902f4bb1501db834e0005919237_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-ad95e902f4bb1501db834e0005919237-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Aspiring Pro Heroes undergo special education during their high school careers and receive licenses that give them the authority to use their Quirks freely.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Quirk_Types">Quirk Types</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Known_Quirk_Types">Known Quirk Types</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Emitter">Emitter</span></h4>
<p><b>Emitter</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">発動</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><i>Hatsudō</i></span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>,  lit. "Activation")</span>-type Quirks are abilities that allow the user to generate and possibly control certain things, or alter existing things around them in certain ways. The emissions of Emitter-type Quirks can have a wide variety of properties and abilities.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/12/Denki_Beats_Bots.png/revision/latest?cb=20170716181804" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Denki Beats Bots.png" data-image-key="Denki_Beats_Bots.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/12/Denki_Beats_Bots.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170716181804" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/12/Denki_Beats_Bots.png/revision/latest?cb=20170716181804" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/12/Denki_Beats_Bots.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170716181804" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Denki Beats Bots.png" data-image-key="Denki_Beats_Bots.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/1/12/Denki_Beats_Bots.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20170716181804" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Denki_Beats_Bots.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Denki_Kaminari" title="Denki Kaminari">Denki Kaminari</a> emitting <a href="/wiki/Electrification" title="Electrification">electricity</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Emitter-type Quirks, such as <a href="/wiki/Brainwashing" title="Brainwashing">Brainwashing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Explosion" title="Explosion">Explosion</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Half-Cold_Half-Hot" title="Half-Cold Half-Hot">Half-Cold Half-Hot</a> usually require a conscious effort to activate, and some, such as <a href="/wiki/Erasure" title="Erasure">Erasure</a>, even require large amounts of concentration in order for them to remain active.
</p><p>Emitter-type Quirks can also have various ranges. While some users require <a href="/wiki/Zero_Gravity" title="Zero Gravity">physical contact</a> to use them, while others can have much <a href="/wiki/Navel_Laser" title="Navel Laser">longer ranges</a> with no distance restrictions.
</p><p>While most Emitter-type Quirk users generally have a handle on their own "emissions", it's also possible for users to <a href="/wiki/Explosion" title="Explosion">hurt themselves</a> from coming into too much contact with their Quirk. In the case of generating substances, making too much too fast or for too long can harm the user as they are <a href="/wiki/Creation" title="Creation">using reserves</a> from their own body, or gradually lose their natural resistance to their own <a href="/wiki/Acid" title="Acid">harmful Quirk</a>.
</p><p>While some things produced by Emitter-type Quirks, such as the loud sound produced by <a href="/wiki/Voice" title="Voice">Voice</a>, have common properties, some are unique to the user, and thus have special properties, such as the ectoplasm produced by <a href="/wiki/Clones" title="Clones">Clones</a>. Those who alter the properties of things around them can also widely vary in effects, from <a href="/wiki/Softening" title="Softening">molecular alteration</a> to <a href="/wiki/Decay" title="Decay">molecular destruction</a>.
</p><p>Some Emitter-type Quirks cause the user's body to take on a temporary alternation. While such Quirks would normally fall into the Transformation class, the difference is that these powers require the user to take in an outside resource in order for the Quirk to activate. Such Quirks are <a href="/wiki/Sugar_Rush" title="Sugar Rush">Sugar Rush</a>, which requires the user to ingest sugar, and <a href="/wiki/IQ" title="IQ">IQ</a>, which requires the user to drink tea.
</p><p>Emitter-type Quirks are, by a wide margin, the most common type of Quirk.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Transformation">Transformation</span></h4>
<p><b>Transformation</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">変形</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><i>Henkei</i></span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>-type Quirks are abilities that cause the user to take on a temporary alteration of some kind. Transformation-type Quirks allow the user to temporarily "transform" their body in a variety of manners, sometimes <a href="/wiki/Hardening" title="Hardening">enhancing</a> <a href="/wiki/Gigantification" title="Gigantification">existing</a> <a href="/wiki/Pliabody" title="Pliabody">features</a>, removing features, or <a href="/wiki/Razor_Sharp" title="Razor Sharp">adding</a> <a href="/wiki/Muscle_Augmentation" title="Muscle Augmentation">new</a> <a href="/wiki/Spike" title="Spike">features</a> to the body altogether.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/d/d9/Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png/revision/latest?cb=20190520225623" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="211" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lizard Tail Splitter.png" data-image-key="Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/d/d9/Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190520225623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/d/d9/Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png/revision/latest?cb=20190520225623" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/d/d9/Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190520225623" decoding="async" width="220" height="211" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lizard Tail Splitter.png" data-image-key="Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/d/d9/Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20190520225623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lizard_Tail_Splitter.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Setsuna_Tokage" title="Setsuna Tokage">Setsuna Tokage</a> transforming her body into <a href="/wiki/Lizard_Tail_Splitter" title="Lizard Tail Splitter">pieces</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Transformation-type Quirks usually require a conscious effort by the user to "activate", though most users can be trained to initiate them reflexively, depending on the conditions required for activation, and practice to initiate their Quirks with greater intent and precision, such as with <a href="/wiki/Shinya_Kamihara" title="Shinya Kamihara">Edgeshot</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Foldabody" title="Foldabody">Quirk</a>; he's mastered it to a point where he can change in an instant.
</p><p>Transformation-type Quirks usually require a close-range proximity in order to fully utilize them in combat due to them only affecting the user's body. While Transformation-type Quirks are often quite powerful, their biggest weakness is that their effects are often temporary, and over-exertion usually leads to negative repercussions on the user's behalf. Transformation Quirks can also be limited based on the user, how resilient their body is, and the resources they have available to them (Ex. <a href="/wiki/Tetsutetsu_Tetsutetsu" title="Tetsutetsu Tetsutetsu">Tetsutetsu Tetsutetsu</a> describes that his <a href="/wiki/Steel" title="Steel">Steel</a> Quirk softens if he doesn't consume enough Iron, and suffers from Iron Fatigue if he maintains it for too long). Some users condition their body in certain ways so that their Quirks can operate more effectively.
</p><p>Transformation-type Quirks are the only known type of Quirk that can bestow the user attributes they do not normally exhibit by default. Because this type of Quirk combines the activation time and mutant-shape aspects of the other Quirk types, it is also often known as <b>Hybrid</b> or <b>Composite</b>.
</p><p>Transformation-type Quirks generally affect the user exclusively, the only known exception being Seiji Shishikura's <a href="/wiki/Meatball" title="Meatball">Meatball</a>.
</p><p>Transformation seems to be the least common type of Quirk.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mutant">Mutant</span></h4>
<p><b>Mutant</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">異形</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma" style="display:none">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><i>Igyō</i></span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Installing_Japanese_character_sets" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Installing Japanese character sets"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>-type (also called <b>Heteromorphic</b>-type) Quirks are abilities that cause the user a permanent "abnormality" directly related to their power. Mutant-type Quirks create bodily structures that grant the user more complex abilities that Emitter and Transformation Quirks cannot safely provide. Often times they will bestow <a href="/wiki/Tail" title="Tail">prehensile</a> <a href="/wiki/Vines" title="Vines">appendages</a> that the user can control or <a href="/wiki/Tape" title="Tape">add</a> <a href="/wiki/Engine" title="Engine">structures</a> to pre-existing limbs to enhance pre-existing abilities. Mutant-type Quirks even have the ability to <a href="/wiki/Earphone_Jack" title="Earphone Jack">channel certain aspects</a> of their user through them in a similar manner to Emitter-type Quirks.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 222px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6e/Dupli-Arms.png/revision/latest?cb=20180422024043" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="220" height="183" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dupli-Arms.png" data-image-key="Dupli-Arms.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6e/Dupli-Arms.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180422024043" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6e/Dupli-Arms.png/revision/latest?cb=20180422024043" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6e/Dupli-Arms.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180422024043" decoding="async" width="220" height="183" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dupli-Arms.png" data-image-key="Dupli-Arms.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/bokunoheroacademia/images/6/6e/Dupli-Arms.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20180422024043" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dupli-Arms.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Mezo_Shoji" title="Mezo Shoji">Mezo Shoji</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Dupli-Arms" title="Dupli-Arms">mutation</a> gives him extra arms that he can transform into other body parts.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Mutant-type Quirks are also the only known type of Quirk which can be passed down through generations without necessarily bestowing the corresponding ability, such as with <a href="/wiki/Fumikage_Tokoyami" title="Fumikage Tokoyami">Fumikage Tokoyami</a> and his bird-like head that has nothing to do with his <a href="/wiki/Dark_Shadow" title="Dark Shadow">Dark Shadow</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Koji_Koda" title="Koji Koda">Koji Koda</a>'s rock-like head which speaks nothing of his <a href="/wiki/Anivoice" title="Anivoice">Anivoice</a> Quirk. As a result of this, while it's uncertain how common mutant Quirks are, it can be safely assumed they are the most commonly inherited.
</p><p>While not necessarily a weakness, Mutant-type Quirks cannot be turned off, and sometimes cause the user inconvenience due to their malformations. Such is the case with <a href="/wiki/Mashirao_Ojiro" title="Mashirao Ojiro">Mashirao Ojiro</a> and his <a href="/wiki/Tail" title="Tail">Tail</a> Quirk, which makes it difficult for him to sit or lay down, as well as <a href="/wiki/Toru_Hagakure" title="Toru Hagakure">Toru Hagakure</a> and her <a href="/wiki/Invisibility" title="Invisibility">Invisibility</a> Quirk, which makes it impossible to see her reflection or show up in photos. Though because these Quirks are passively-active, they are partially immune to Quirk-disabling effects such as that of <a href="/wiki/Shota_Aizawa" title="Shota Aizawa">Shota Aizawa</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Erasure" title="Erasure">Erasure</a> Quirk. Since Mutant Quirks are passively active they are the most identifiable at a glance.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Known_Quirk_Sub-Types">Known Quirk Sub-Types</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Accumulation">Accumulation</span></h4>
<p>Accumulation-type Quirk's are powers that, in order to function properly, require the user accumulate something ahead of time, such as power, energy, mass, or a particular resource. Some such Quirks are <a href="/wiki/One_For_All" title="One For All">One For All</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stress" title="Stress">Stress</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rewind" title="Rewind">Rewind</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fat_Absorption" title="Fat Absorption">Fat Absorption</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ch217_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ch217-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<th>Unnamed Paranormal Liberation Front Commander
